Both Output (a) and Output (b) provide a Python function to solve this problem.  Output (a) provides a more straightforward and efficient solution. It uses a recursive approach to traverse the binary tree and finds the highest common ancestor by checking if the current node is either of the two nodes or if the left and right subtrees return a non-None value.
